  `id` int(11) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `name` varchar(40) NOT NULL,
  `company` varchar(80) NOT NULL,
  `customer_type` enum('Trade','Institutional','Government') NOT NULL DEFAULT 'Trade',
  `email` varchar(80) NOT NULL,
  `mobile` varchar(40) NOT NULL,
  `tel` varchar(40) NOT NULL,
  `fax` varchar(40) NOT NULL,
  `pan` varchar(40) NOT NULL,
  `vat` varchar(40) NOT NULL,
  `cst` varchar(40) NOT NULL,
  `cst_valid` varchar(40) NOT NULL,
  `bank_name` varchar(40) NOT NULL,
  `bank_branch` varchar(40) NOT NULL,
  `bank_city` varchar(40) NOT NULL,
  `bank_swift_code` varchar(40) NOT NULL,
  `bank_ac_no` varchar(40) NOT NULL,
  `rating` varchar(40) NOT NULL,
  `user_id` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `last_update` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP ON UPDATE CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB  DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1 AUTO_INCREMENT=164 ;

--
-- Table structure for table `spl_customer_discount_master`
--

CREATE TABLE `spl_customer_discount_master` (
  `id` int(11) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `name` varchar(40) NOT NULL,
  `remarks` varchar(80) NOT NULL,

  `percentage` float NOT NULL,

) ENGINE=InnoDB  DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1 AUTO_INCREMENT=26 ;

-- Table structure for table `spl_invoice_master`
--

  `id` int(11) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `order_id` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `customer_address_id` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `challan_no` varchar(40) NOT NULL,
  `challan_date` date NOT NULL,
  `devilery_date` date NOT NULL,
  `payment_mode` varchar(40) NOT NULL,
  `despatch_no` varchar(40) NOT NULL,
  `despatch_date` date NOT NULL,
  `despatch_through` varchar(40) NOT NULL,
  `devilery_terms` varchar(40) NOT NULL,
  `destination` varchar(40) NOT NULL,
  `invoice_date` date NOT NULL,
  `status` enum('Open','Closed') NOT NULL DEFAULT 'Open',
  `user_id` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `last_update` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP ON UPDATE CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB  DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1 AUTO_INCREMENT=679 ;

--
-- Table structure for table `spl_order_master`
--

CREATE TABLE `spl_order_master` (
  `id` int(11) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `customer_id` int(11) DEFAULT NULL,
  `prefered_delivery_date` date DEFAULT NULL,
  `reference` varchar(80) DEFAULT NULL,

  `id` int(11) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `order_id` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `tax_discount_id` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `type` enum('Discount','Tax') NOT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  UNIQUE KEY `id` (`id`),
  UNIQUE KEY `order_id_2` (`order_id`,`tax_discount_id`),
  KEY `order_id` (`order_id`,`tax_discount_id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB  DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1 AUTO_INCREMENT=1533 ;

-- --------------------------------------------------------

--
-- Table structure for table `spl_package_master`
--

CREATE TABLE `spl_package_master` (
  `id` int(11) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `volume` float NOT NULL,
  `unit_type` enum('ml','mg') NOT NULL DEFAULT 'ml',
  `quantity_in_box` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `type` enum('Plastic','Glass','Gallon') NOT NULL DEFAULT 'Plastic',
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  UNIQUE KEY `id` (`id`),
  KEY `id_2` (`id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB  DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1 AUTO_INCREMENT=11 ;

-- Dumping data for table `spl_package_master`
--

-- --------------------------------------------------------

--
-- Table structure for table `spl_price_master`
--

CREATE TABLE `spl_price_master` (
  `id` int(11) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `product_id` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `package_id` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `customer_type` enum('Trade','Institutional','Government') NOT NULL,
  `unit_price` float NOT NULL,
  `mrp` float NOT NULL,
  `status` tinyint(4) NOT NULL DEFAULT '1',
  `valid_from` date NOT NULL,
  `valid_to` date NOT NULL,
  `last_update` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP ON UPDATE CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB  DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1 AUTO_INCREMENT=149 ;

-- Table structure for table `spl_product_master`
--

  `id` int(11) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `name` varchar(80) NOT NULL,
  `short_code` varchar(80) NOT NULL,
  `type` varchar(80) NOT NULL,
  `unit` enum('ml','mg') NOT NULL DEFAULT 'ml',
  `tariff_sub_heading` varchar(40) NOT NULL DEFAULT '30045020',
  `status` tinyint(4) NOT NULL DEFAULT '1',
  `last_update` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP ON UPDATE CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB  DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1 AUTO_INCREMENT=31 ;

  `id` int(11) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `order_id` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `customer_id` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `total_amount` float NOT NULL,
  `central_excise_duty` float NOT NULL,

  `bill_amount` float NOT NULL,

  UNIQUE KEY `order_id` (`order_id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB  DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1 AUTO_INCREMENT=484 ;

--
-- Table structure for table `spl_stock_ledger`
--

CREATE TABLE `spl_stock_ledger` (
  `id` int(11) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `product_id` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `package_id` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `mfg_date` date NOT NULL,
  `exp_date` varchar(40) NOT NULL,
  `batch_id` enum('L','S') NOT NULL DEFAULT 'L',
  `batch_no` int(4) unsigned zerofill NOT NULL,
  `location` varchar(40) NOT NULL,
  `transaction_date` date NOT NULL,
  `transaction_reference_no` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `quantity` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `transaction_type` enum('Production','Sale','Transfer-in','Transfer-out','Transfer-pending','Stock_correction') NOT NULL,
  `remarks` varchar(80) NOT NULL,
  `user_id` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `last_update` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP ON UPDATE CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  UNIQUE KEY `id` (`id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB  DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1 AUTO_INCREMENT=2593 ;

-- Table structure for table `spl_stock_master`

  `id` int(11) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `product_id` int(11) NOT NULL,

  `available_unit` int(11) NOT NULL,

  `location` varchar(80) NOT NULL,
  `transaction_type` enum('Production','Sale','Transfer-in','Transfer-out','Transfer-pending','Stock_correction') NOT NULL,
  `user_id` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `last_update` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP ON UPDATE CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,

  `id` int(11) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,

  `catagory` varchar(40) NOT NULL,
  `percentage` float NOT NULL,
  `status` tinyint(4) NOT NULL DEFAULT '1',
  `valid_from` date NOT NULL,
  `valid_to` date NOT NULL,
  `last_update` timestamp NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP ON UPDATE CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB  DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1 AUTO_INCREMENT=2001 ;
